Keywords and source-specific queries live in `config.json`.

## Local Update

```bash
python scripts/update_papers.py
```

Generated files:

- `README.md`
- `data/papers.json`
- `data/papers.csv`
- `data/run_summary.json`
- `data/graph.json`
